<a id="10377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9485" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10384" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10386" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10390" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10390" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="10393" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1963" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10395" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="10397" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="10403" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="10406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9485" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10384" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10386" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10390" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="10421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1963" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#9485" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="10430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10384" class="Bound">Σ</a> <a id="10432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10386" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="10435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#10395" class="Bound">⊢M</a>

<a id="10439" class="Comment">{-
⊢subst : ∀ {Γ Δ xs ys ρ}
  → (∀ {x}   → x ∈ xs       →  free (ρ x) ⊆ ys)
  → (∀ {x A} → x ∈ xs       →  Γ ∋ x ⦂ A  →  Δ ⊢ ρ x ⦂ A)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
  → (∀ {M A} → free M ⊆ xs  →  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A  →  Δ ⊢ subst ys ρ M ⦂ A)
⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (` ⊢x)
    =  ⊢ρ (⊆xs here) ⊢x
⊢subst {Γ} {Δ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (`λ_ {x = x} {A = A} {N = N} ⊢N)
    = `λ_ {x = y} {A = A} (⊢subst {Γ′} {Δ′} {xs′} {ys′} {ρ′} Σ′ ⊢ρ′ ⊆xs′ ⊢N)
  where
  y   =  fresh ys
  Γ′  =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  Δ′  =  Δ , y ⦂ A
  xs′ =  x ∷ xs
  ys′ =  y ∷ ys
  ρ′  =  ρ , x ↦ ` y

  Σ′ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs′ →  free (ρ′ w) ⊆ ys′
  Σ′ {w} w∈′ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes refl    =  ⊆-++₁
  ...            | no  w≢      =  ⊆-++₂ ∘ Σ (there⁻¹ w∈′ w≢)
  
  ⊆xs′ :  free N ⊆ xs′
  ⊆xs′ =  \\-to-∷ ⊆xs

  ⊢σ : ∀ {w C} → w ∈ ys → Δ ∋ w ⦂ C → Δ′ ∋ w ⦂ C
  ⊢σ w∈ ⊢w  =  S (fresh-lemma w∈) ⊢w

  ⊢ρ′ : ∀ {w C} → w ∈ xs′ → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ C → Δ′ ⊢ ρ′ w ⦂ C
  ⊢ρ′ {w} _ Z with w ≟ x
  ...         | yes _             =  ` Z
  ...         | no  w≢            =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ′ {w} w∈′ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...         | yes refl          =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...         | no  _             =  ⊢rename {Δ} {Δ′} {ys} ⊢σ (Σ w∈) (⊢ρ w∈ ⊢w)
              where
              w∈  =  there⁻¹ w∈′ w≢

⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ ⊆xs (⊢L · ⊢M)
    =  ⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ L⊆ ⊢L · ⊢subst Σ ⊢ρ M⊆ ⊢M
  where
  L⊆ = trans-⊆ ⊆-++₁ ⊆xs
  M⊆ = trans-⊆ ⊆-++₂ ⊆xs
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="12431" class="Comment">---------------</a>
  <a id="12449" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12381" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12386" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12388" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="12461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12368" class="Function">⊢weaker</a> <a id="12469" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12471" class="Symbol">{!!}</a>

  <a id="12512" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#7026" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="12518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12497" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Collections.md %}{% raw %}#1762" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="12522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#4393" class="Function">free</a> <a id="12527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12507" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12529" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.List.Base.html#1336" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="12532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12533" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#4393" class="Function">free</a> <a id="12538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12503" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Collections.md %}{% raw %}#1835" class="Function Operator">\\</a> <a id="12543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12499" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12544" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12548" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12497" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1394" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12499" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1394" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12501" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12503" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12505" class="Bound">B</a>

    <a id="12586" class="Comment">---------------------</a>
  <a id="12610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12497" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="12614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12503" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="12618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5373" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="12620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12499" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5373" class="Function Operator">:=</a> <a id="12625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12507" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#5373" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="12629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#1735" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="12631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12505" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="12633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBadfix.md %}{% raw %}#12477" class="Function">⊢substitution₀</a> <a id="12648" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12650" class="Symbol">{!!}</a>

<a id="12656" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M}
  → Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B
  → Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A
    --------------------
  → Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  ⊢weaker {Γ} {ys} ⊆N[x:=M]
    (⊢substitution₀
      (refl-⊆ (//-lemma {Γ} {ys}))
      (⊢stronger {Γ , x ⦂ A} {x ∷ ys} ⊆N ⊢N)
      (⊢stronger {Γ} {ys} ⊆M ⊢M))
    where
    ys = free M ++ (free N \\ x)
    ⊆N : free N ⊆ x ∷ ys
    ⊆N = ?
    ⊆M : free M ⊆ ys
    ⊆M = ?
    ⊆N[x:=M] : free (N [ x := M ]) ⊆ ys
    ⊆N[x:=M] = ?
-}</a>
  
<a id="13159" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  subst {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊢N′
  where
  ys   =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  Δ    =  Γ // ys
  ⊢N′  =  rename {Γ , x ⦂ A} {Δ , x ⦂ A} ? ⊢N
  ⊢M′  =  rename {Γ} {Δ} ? ⊢M
  
  -- rename is no longer sufficiently powerful
  -- it can do weakening but not strengthening

  -- not clear where and how def&#39;n of ys gets used

  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>

<a id="14328" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  subst {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ ⊢N′
  where
  ys   =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  Γ′   =  Γ // ys
  ⊢N′  =  rename {Γ , x ⦂ A} {Γ′ , x ⦂ A} ? ⊢N
  ⊢M′  =  rename {Γ} {Γ′} ? ⊢M
  
  -- rename is no longer sufficiently powerful
  -- it can do weakening but not strengthening

  -- not clear where and how def&#39;n of ys gets used

  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>

<a id="15499" class="Comment">{-
⊢substitution : ∀ {Γ x A N B M} →
  Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ⦂ B →
  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A →
  --------------------
  Γ ⊢ N [ x := M ] ⦂ B
⊢substitution {Γ} {x} {A} {N} {B} {M} ⊢N ⊢M =
  ⊢subst {Γ′} {Γ} {xs} {ys} {ρ} Σ ⊢ρ {N} {B} ⊆xs ⊢N
  where
  Γ′     =  Γ , x ⦂ A
  xs     =  free N
  ys     =  free M ++ (free N \\ x)
  ρ      =  ∅ , x ↦ M

  Σ : ∀ {w} → w ∈ xs → free (ρ w) ⊆ ys
  Σ {w} w∈ y∈ with w ≟ x
  ...            | yes _                   =  ⊆-++₁ y∈
  ...            | no w≢ rewrite ∈-[_] y∈  =  ⊆-++₂ (∈-≢-to-\\ w∈ w≢)
  
  ⊢ρ : ∀ {w B} → w ∈ xs → Γ′ ∋ w ⦂ B → Γ ⊢ ρ w ⦂ B
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ Z         with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes _     =  ⊢M
  ...                    | no  w≢    =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ⊢ρ {w} w∈ (S w≢ ⊢w) with w ≟ x
  ...                    | yes refl  =  ⊥-elim (w≢ refl)
  ...                    | no  _     =  ` ⊢w

  ⊆xs : free N ⊆ xs
  ⊆xs x∈ = x∈
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Preservation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16416" class="Comment">{-
preservation : ∀ {Γ M N A}
  →  Γ ⊢ M ⦂ A
  →  M ⟶ N
     ---------
  →  Γ ⊢ N ⦂ A
preservation (` ⊢x) ()
preservation (`λ ⊢N) ()
preservation (⊢L · ⊢M) (ξ-⟹₁ L⟶L′)        =  preservation ⊢L L⟶L′ · ⊢M
preservation (⊢V · ⊢M) (ξ-⟹₂ valV M⟶M′)   =  ⊢V · preservation ⊢M M⟶M′
preservation ((`λ ⊢N) · ⊢W) (β-⟹ valW)      =  ⊢substitution ⊢N ⊢W
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
